# Voynich Phytoglyphica — Complete Entry Listing

Complete enumeration of all pharmaceutical and procedural entries
derived from the Voynich Manuscript (VMS) via the Imscribing Grammar engine.

- **Part I — Botanical/Pharmaceutical Entries:** 1,491
- **Part II — Procedural Recipes:** 1,076

Folio identification status: **[confirmed]** = one of 35 IG-catalogued plants;
**[proposed]** = scholarly candidate identification from medieval herbal tradition.

Fields — Part I: folio · para · preparatio · forma · potentia · pars_plantae · applicatio · volatilis · fixatio · indicatio · n_ops
Fields — Part II: folio · para · n_ops · n_steps · steps (Accipe steps carry named botanical ingredients)

---

## Part II — Procedural Recipes (1,076)

### f103r — Procedural recipe register (Multi-ingredient preparation folio) · Recipe section [recipe section]

**Entry 1 — f103r/p01** · n_ops=13 · n_steps=11

- Step 1: Divide/tere (Divide or grind)
- Step 2: Calefac/commisce (Heat or combine)
- Step 3: Divide/tere (Divide or grind)
- Step 4: Accipe materiam — Artemisia absinthium (f1r)
- Step 5: Calefac/commisce (Heat or combine)
- Step 6: Accipe 2 materias — Pimpinella anisum (f40v), Papaver rhoeas (f4v)
- Step 7: Calefac ×2 (Heat/mix 2 times)
- Step 8: Extrahe/colare (Extract or strain)
- Step 9: Accipe materiam — Achillea millefolium (f28r)
- Step 10: Extrahe/colare (Extract or strain)
- Step 11: Compone (Compose/formulate final mixture)

**Entry 2 — f103r/p02** · n_ops=15 · n_steps=15

- Step 1: Extrahe/colare (Extract or strain)
- Step 2: Calefac/commisce (Heat or combine)
- Step 3: Divide/tere (Divide or grind)
- Step 4: Accipe materiam — Carlina acaulis (f52v)
- Step 5: Divide/tere (Divide or grind)
- Step 6: Calefac/commisce (Heat or combine)
- Step 7: Divide/tere (Divide or grind)
- Step 8: Extrahe/colare (Extract or strain)
- Step 9: Divide/tere (Divide or grind)
- Step 10: Extrahe/colare (Extract or strain)
- Step 11: Applica/administra (Apply or administer)
